021002,003569:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
021003,003570: 
021004,003571:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
021005,003572:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR. THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
021006,003573:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
021007,003574:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
021008,003575: 
021009,003576:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
021010,003577:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.    1) BY ENDIDLE
021011,003578:                                                                                                  #              2) BY NVSUBUSY
021012,003579:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
021013,003580:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME. IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
021014,003581:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY A JOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
021015,003582:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
021016,003583: 
021017,003584: 
021018,003585:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
021019,003586:                                                                                                  #           CAF    V/N
021020,003587:                                                                                                  #  L        TC     NVSUB
021021,003588:                                                                                                  #  L+1      RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
021022,003589:                                                                                                  #  L+2      RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
021023,003590: 
021024,003591: 
021025,003592:                                                                                                  #        A ROUTINE CALLED  NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL)  TO PUT
021026,003593:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
021027,003594:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM. NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
021028,003595:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
021029,003596:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
021030,003597: 
021031,003598: 
021032,003599:                                                                                                  #         THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
021033,003600:                                                                                                  #           CAF    WAKEFCADR
021034,003601:                                                                                                  #           TC     NVSUBUSY
021035,003602: 
021036,003603: 
021037,003604:                                                                                                  #  .
021038,003605: 
021039,003606: 
021040,003607:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
021041,003608:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
021042,003609:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
021043,003610:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
021044,003611: 
021045,003612: 
021046,003613:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
021047,003614:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
021048,003615:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
021049,003616:                                                                                                  #  1) DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
021050,003617:                                                                                                  #     IS EXCEEDED.
021051,003618:                                                                                                  #  2) CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 477 

021053,003620:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
021054,003621: 
021055,003622:    4437           44444        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
021056,003623:    4440           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF(LOC
021057,003624:    4441           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
021058,003625:    4442           04635        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
021059,003626:    4443           10604                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
021060,003627:    4444           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
021061,003628: 
021062,003629:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
021063,003630:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
021064,003631: 
021065,003632: 04,2604                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
021066,003633: 04,2604                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
021067,003634: 04,2604           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
021068,003635: 04,2605           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
021069,003636: 04,2606           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
021070,003637: 04,2607           04374                           TC       RELDSPON                              
021071,003638: 04,2610           30001                           CA       L                                     
021072,003639: 04,2611           55043                           TS       DSPLIST                               
021073,003640: 04,2612           05133        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
021074,003641: 
021075,003642: 
021076,003643:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
021077,003644:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
021078,003645:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE). IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
021079,003646:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
021080,003647:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
021081,003648: 
021082,003649:    4445                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
021083,003650:    4445                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
021084,003651:    4445           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
021085,003652:    4446           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
021086,003653:    4447           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
021087,003654:    4450           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
021088,003655:    4451           61012                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
021089,003656:    4452           10000                           CCS      A                                     
021090,003657:    4453           14455                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
021091,003658:    4454           14164                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
021092,003659:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.
021093,003660:    4455           24002        NVSBWT1            INCR     Q                                     #  L+2. PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
021094,003661:    4456           14437                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
021095,003662: 
021096,003663: 
021097,003664:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP IS USED BY VBPROC, VBTERM, VBRQEXEC, VBRQWAIT, VBRELDSP, EXTENDED
021098,003665:                                                                                                  #  VERB DISPATCHER, VBRESEQ, RECALTST.
021099,003666:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP1 IS USED BY MONITOR SET UP, VBRELDSP.

021248,003815:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF,
021249,003816:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
021250,003817:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
021251,003818:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
021252,003819:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROES THE :TEST ALARM: OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY,RESTART.
021253,003820:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS :CAUTION RESET: TO 1.
